[User Routine     ] : QUOTES
[User Routine Text] :
/SAPDMC/LSRATT                DAI_PM         URQUOTES                              000     000                                                                                                0101KGONUGUNTLA 20180404
/SAPDMC/LSRTXT                EDAI_PM         URQUOTES
/SAPDMC/LSRCOD                DAI_PM         URQUOTES                        0001* Eigene Routine
/SAPDMC/LSRCOD                DAI_PM         URQUOTES                        0002form ur_QUOTES
/SAPDMC/LSRCOD                DAI_PM         URQUOTES                        0003     using p_in
/SAPDMC/LSRCOD                DAI_PM         URQUOTES                        0004  changing p_out.
/SAPDMC/LSRCOD                DAI_PM         URQUOTES                        0005  DATA: l_len TYPE i.
/SAPDMC/LSRCOD                DAI_PM         URQUOTES                        0006  IF p_in+0(1) = '"'.
/SAPDMC/LSRCOD                DAI_PM         URQUOTES                        0007    REPLACE '"' IN p_in WITH space.
/SAPDMC/LSRCOD                DAI_PM         URQUOTES                        0008    CONDENSE p_in+0(1).
/SAPDMC/LSRCOD                DAI_PM         URQUOTES                        0009  ENDIF.
/SAPDMC/LSRCOD                DAI_PM         URQUOTES                        0010  l_len = STRLEN( p_in ).
/SAPDMC/LSRCOD                DAI_PM         URQUOTES                        0011  IF l_len GT 0.
/SAPDMC/LSRCOD                DAI_PM         URQUOTES                        0012    l_len = l_len - 1.
/SAPDMC/LSRCOD                DAI_PM         URQUOTES                        0013    IF p_in+l_len(1) = '"'.
/SAPDMC/LSRCOD                DAI_PM         URQUOTES                        0014      REPLACE '"' IN p_in WITH space.
/SAPDMC/LSRCOD                DAI_PM         URQUOTES                        0015      CONDENSE p_in+l_len(1).
/SAPDMC/LSRCOD                DAI_PM         URQUOTES                        0016    ENDIF.
/SAPDMC/LSRCOD                DAI_PM         URQUOTES                        0017  ENDIF.
/SAPDMC/LSRCOD                DAI_PM         URQUOTES                        0018  p_out = p_in.
/SAPDMC/LSRCOD                DAI_PM         URQUOTES                        0019ENDFORM.
